<h1 _ngcontent-hqa-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="属性"> 属性 </h1>

<div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>通用属性仅支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-layout-constraints#aspectratio">aspectRatio</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backdropblur">backdropBlur</a>、<a class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>该组件首批接口从API version 8开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>示例效果请以真机运行为准，当前DevEco Studio预览器不支持。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1242px;">     <h2 id="domstorageaccess" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">domStorageAccess<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="domstorageaccess" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>domStorageAccess(domStorageAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启文档对象模型存储接口（DOM Storage API）权限，当属性没有显式调用时，默认不开启文档对象模型存储接口（DOM Storage API）权限。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">domStorageAccess</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否开启文档对象模型存储接口（DOM Storage API）权限。</p>          <p>true表示开启文档对象模型存储接口权限，false表示不开启文档对象模型存储接口权限。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>网页中使用到文档对象模型存储接口（DOM Storage API），需将其设置为true，才可正常加载网页。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fileAccess<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fileaccess" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fileAccess(fileAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启应用中文件系统的访问。<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/resource-categories-and-access" target="_blank">$rawfile(filepath/filename)</a>中的文件不受该属性影响而被限制访问。API version 11及以前，当属性没有显式调用时，默认开启应用中文件系统的访问。API version 12及以后，当属性没有显式调用时，默认不开启应用中文件系统的访问。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">fileAccess</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否开启应用中文件系统的访问。</p>          <p>true表示开启应用中文件系统的访问。false表示不开启应用中文件系统的访问。</p>          <p>同时，当fileAccess为false的时候，仅只读资源目录/data/storage/el1/bundle/entry/resources/resfile里面的资源依然可以通过file协议访问，不受fileAccess管控。</p>          <p>API version 11及以前，传入undefined或null时为true，API version 12及以后传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">imageAccess<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="imageaccess" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>imageAccess(imageAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否允许自动加载图片资源。当属性没有显式调用时，允许自动加载图片资源。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">imageAccess</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否允许自动加载图片资源。</p>          <p>true表示设置允许自动加载图片资源，false表示设置不允许自动加载图片资源。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">javaScriptProxy<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="javascriptproxy" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>javaScriptProxy(javaScriptProxy: JavaScriptProxy)</p>     <p>将javaScriptProxy中的ArkTS对象注册到Web组件中，该对象将使用JavaScriptProxy中指定的名称注册到网页的所有框架中，包括所有iframe，这使得JavaScript可以调用javaScriptProxy中ArkTS对象的方法。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将javaScriptProxy中的ArkTS对象注册到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>javaScriptProxy接口需要和deleteJavaScriptRegister接口配合使用，防止内存泄漏。</p>       <p>javaScriptProxy对象的所有参数不支持更新。</p>       <p>注册javaScriptProxy对象时，同步与异步列表请至少选择一项不为空，可同时注册两类方法。</p>       <p>此接口只支持注册一个对象，若需要注册多个对象请使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-webview-webviewcontroller#registerjavascriptproxy">registerJavaScriptProxy<sup>9+</sup></a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr> class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>javaScriptAccess(javaScriptAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否允许执行JavaScript脚本。当属性没有显式调用时，默认允许执行JavaScript脚本。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div id="overscrollmode11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">overScrollMode<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="overscrollmode11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>overScrollMode(mode: OverScrollMode)</p>     <p>设置Web过滚动模式。当过滚动模式开启时，当用户在Web根页面上滑动到边缘时，Web会通过弹性动画弹回界面，根页面上的内部页面不会触发回弹。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#overscrollmode11">OverScrollMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置Web的过滚动模式为关闭或开启。</p>          <p>默认值：OverScrollMode.NEVER，表示关闭过滚动模式。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 998px;">     <h2 id="mixedmode" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">mixedMode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mixedmode" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>mixedMode(mixedMode: MixedMode)</p>     <p>设定当安全源尝试从非安全源加载资源时的行为。当属性没有显式调用时，默认值为MixedMode.None，即禁止安全源从非安全源加载内容。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1094px;">     <h2 id="onlineimageaccess" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onlineImageAccess<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onlineimageaccess" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onlineImageAccess(onlineImageAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否允许从网络加载图片资源（通过HTTP和HTTPS访问的资源）。当属性没有显式调用时，默认允许从网络加载图片资源。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置有声视频的自动播放是否需要用户手动点击。</p>          <p>true表示设置有声视频的自动播放需要用户手动点击，false表示设置有声视频的自动播放不需要用户手动点击，能自动播放。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">multiWindowAccess<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">multiWindow</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2270px;">     <h2 id="horizontalscrollbaraccess9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">horizontalScrollBarAccess<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>horizontalScrollBarAccess(horizontalScrollBar: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否显示横向滚动条，包括系统默认滚动条和用户自定义滚动条。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>通过@State变量控制横向滚动条的隐藏/显示后，需要调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-webview-webviewcontroller#refresh">controller.refresh()</a>生效。</li>        <li>通过@State变量频繁动态改变时，建议切换开关变量和Web组件一一对应。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">horizontalScrollBar</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否显示横向滚动条。</p>          <p>true表示设置显示横向滚动条，false表示设置不显示横向滚动条。</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> id="defaultfixedfontsize9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">defaultFixedFontSize<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="defaultfixedfontsize9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>defaultFixedFontSize(size: number)</p>     <p>设置网页的默认等宽字体大小。对于html前端使用monospace字体且未指定font-size样式的元素，将按此值渲染字体大小。</p>     <p>当属性没有显式调用时，默认等宽字体大小为13。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置网页的默认等宽字体大小，单位px。</p>          <p>输入值的范围为[-2^31, 2^31-1]，实际渲染时超过72px的值按照72px进行渲染，低于1px的值按照1px进行渲染。</p>          <p>传入null或undefined时为13。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minLogicalFontSize(size: number)</p>     <p>设置网页逻辑字体大小最小值。</p>     <p>对于html前端未指定font-size样式的元素：</p>     <ol>      <li>若元素字体大小低于该接口设置值，将采用接口设置值渲染字体大小。</li>      <li>若minLogicalFontSize和minFontSize同时设置时，对于未指定font-size样式元素，将采用两者中的较大值。</li>     </ol>     <p>当属性没有显式调用时，默认网页逻辑字体大小最小值为8。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置网页逻辑字体大小最小值，单位px。</p>          <p>输入值的范围为[-2^31, 2^31-1]，实际渲染时超过72px的值按照72px进行渲染，低于1px的值按照1px进行渲染。</p>          <p>传入null或undefined时为18。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div auto 1046px;">     <h2 id="darkmode9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">darkMode<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="darkmode9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>darkMode(mode: WebDarkMode)</p>     <p>设置Web深色模式。当属性没有显式调用时，默认Web深色模式关闭。</p>     <p>当深色模式开启时，Web将启用媒体查询prefers-color-scheme中网页所定义的深色样式，若网页未定义深色样式，则保持原状。如需开启强制深色模式，建议配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#forcedarkaccess9">forceDarkAccess</a>使用。深色模式具体用法可参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/web-set-dark-mode" target="_blank">Web深色模式适配</a>。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#webdarkmode9">WebDarkMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置Web的深色模式为关闭、开启或跟随系统。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" xxx.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { webview } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkWeb'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Entry</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Component</span></li><li>struct <span class="hljs-title class_">WebComponent</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">controller</span>: webview.<span class="hljs-property">WebviewController</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> webview.<span class="hljs-title class_">WebviewController</span>();</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">build</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-title class_">Column</span>() {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-title class_">Web</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'www.example.com'</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">controller</span>: <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">controller</span> })</li><li>        .<span class="hljs-title function_">pinchSmooth</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">true</span>)</li><li>    }</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3270px;">     <h2 id="allowwindowopenmethod10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">allowWindowOpenMethod<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="allowwindowopenmethod10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>allowWindowOpenMethod(flag: boolean)</p>     <p>设置网页是否可以通过JavaScript自动打开新窗口。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>该属性仅在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#javascriptaccess">javaScriptAccess</a>开启时生效。</li>        <li>该属性在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#multiwindowaccess9">multiWindowAccess</a>开启时打开新窗口，关闭时打开本地窗口。</li>        <li>该属性的默认值与系统属性persist.web.allowWindowOpenMethod.enabled保持一致，如果未设置系统属性则默认值为false。</li>        <li>通过hdc shell param get persist.web.allowWindowOpenMethod.enabled 检查是否开启系统属性persist.web.allowWindowOpenMethod.enabled。若属性值为1代表开启系统属性；若属性值为0或不存在，代表未开启系统属性，可通过命令hdc shell param set persist.web.allowWindowOpenMethod.enabled 1 开启系统属性。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">flag</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>true表示网页可以通过JavaScript自动打开新窗口，该属性为false时，用户行为仍可通过JavaScript自动打开新窗口，但非用户行为不能通过JavaScript自动打开新窗口。</p>          <p>此处的用户行为是指，在用户对Web组件进行点击等操作后，同时在5秒内请求打开新窗口（window.open）的行为。</p>          <p>默认值与系统属性关联，当系统属性persist.web.allowWindowOpenMethod.enabled为true时，默认值为true，如果未设置系统属性则默认值为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1290px;">     <h2 id="mediaoptions10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">mediaOptions<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mediaoptions10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>mediaOptions(options: WebMediaOptions)</p>     <p>设置Web媒体播放的策略，其中包括：Web中的音频在重新获焦后能够自动续播的有效期、应用内多个Web实例的音频是否独占。当该属性未显式设置时，默认Web中的音频重新获焦后无法自动续播、应用内多个Web实例的音频是独占的。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>同一Web实例中的多个音频均视为同一音频。</li>        <li>该媒体播放策略将同时管控有声视频。</li>        <li>建议为所有Web组件设置相同的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#webmediaoptions10">audioExclusive</a>值。</li>        <li>音视频互相打断在应用内和应用间生效，续播只在应用间生效。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.38.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#webmediaoptions10">WebMediaOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置Web的媒体策略。</p>          <p>属性参数更新后需重新播放音频方可生效。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为{resumeInterval: 0, audioExclusive: true}</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// xxx.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { webview } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkWeb'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Entry</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Component</span></li><li>struct <span class="hljs-title class_">WebComponent</span> {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">controller</span>: webview.<span class="hljs-property">WebviewController</span> = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> webview.<span class="hljs-title class_">WebviewController</span>();</li><li>  <span class="hljs-meta">@State</span> <span class="hljs-attr">options</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">WebMediaOptions</span> = {<span class="hljs-attr">resumeInterval</span>: <span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">audioExclusive</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>};</li><li>
</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">build</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-title class_">Column</span>() {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-title language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">controller</span> })</li><li>        .<span class="hljs-title function_">mediaOptions</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">options</span>)</li><li>    }</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2118px;">     <h2 id="javascriptondocumentstart11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">javaScriptOnDocumentStart<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="javascriptondocumentstart11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>javaScriptOnDocumentStart(scripts: Array&lt;ScriptItem&gt;)</p>     <p>将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中，当指定页面或者文档开始加载时，该脚本将在其来源与scriptRules匹配的任何页面中执行。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>网页文档根元素（HTML Element）创建后、但尚未加载任何其他内容之前注入脚本。</p></li>        <li>         <p>该脚本按照字典序执行，非数组本身顺序，若需数组本身顺序，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#runjavascriptondocumentstart15">runJavaScriptOnDocumentStart</a>接口。</p></li>        <li>         <p>不建议与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#runjavascriptondocumentstart15">runJavaScriptOnDocumentStart</a>同时使用。</p></li>        <li>         <p>内容相同的脚本多次注入时将被静默去重，不展示，不提醒，使用首次注入时的scriptRules。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1806px;">     <h2 id="javascriptondocumentend11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">javaScriptOnDocumentEnd<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="javascriptondocumentend11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>javaScriptOnDocumentEnd(scripts: Array&lt;ScriptItem&gt;)</p>     <p>将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中，当指定页面或者文档加载完成时，该脚本将在其来源与scriptRules匹配的任何页面中执行。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>该脚本将在页面的任何JavaScript代码之后运行，并且DOM树此时已经加载、渲染完毕。</p></li>        <li>         <p>该脚本按照字典序执行，非数组本身顺序。</p></li>        <li>         <p>不建议与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#runjavascriptondocumentend15">runJavaScriptOnDocumentEnd</a>同时使用。</p></li>        <li>         <p>内容相同的脚本多次注入时将被静默去重，不展示，不提醒，使用首次注入时的scriptRules。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.40.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">scripts</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#scriptitem11">ScriptItem</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>需要注入的ScriptItem数组。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="runjavascriptondocumentstart15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>runJavaScriptOnDocumentStart(scripts: Array&lt;ScriptItem&gt;)</p>     <p>将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中，当指定页面或者文档开始加载时，该脚本将在其来源与scriptRules匹配的任何页面中执行。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>网页文档根元素（HTML Element）创建后、但尚未加载任何其他内容之前注入脚本。</p></li>        <li>         <p>该脚本按照数组本身顺序执行。</p></li>        <li>         <p>不建议与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#javascriptondocumentstart11">javaScriptOnDocumentStart</a>同时使用。</p></li>        <li>         <p>内容相同的脚本多次注入时将被静默去重，不展示，不提醒，使用首次注入时的scriptRules。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1806px;">     <h2 id="runjavascriptondocumentend15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">runJavaScriptOnDocumentEnd<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="runjavascriptondocumentend15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>runJavaScriptOnDocumentEnd(scripts: Array&lt;ScriptItem&gt;)</p>     <p>将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中，当指定页面或者文档加载完成时，该脚本将在其来源与scriptRules匹配的任何页面中执行。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>         <p>该脚本将在页面的任何JavaScript代码之后运行，并且DOM树此时已经加载、渲染完毕。</p></li>        <li>         <p>该脚本按照数组本身顺序执行。</p></li>        <li>         <p>不建议与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#javascriptondocumentend11">javaScriptOnDocumentEnd</a>同时使用。</p></li>        <li>         <p>内容相同的脚本多次注入时将被静默去重，不展示，不提醒，使用首次注入时的scriptRules。</p></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">scripts</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#scriptitem11">ScriptItem</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>需要注入的ScriptItem数组。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span Array&lt;ScriptItem&gt;)</p>     <p>将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中，当页面DOM树head标签解析完成时，该脚本将在其来源与scriptRules匹配的任何页面中执行。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不将JavaScript脚本注入到Web组件中。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="hljs-string">"utf-8"</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">head</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">body</span> <span class="hljs-attr">style</span>=<span class="hljs-string">"font-size: 30px;"</span>&gt;</span></li><li>Hello world!</li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">"result"</span>&gt;</span>test msg<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">body</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2070px;">     <h2 id="layoutmode11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">layoutMode<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="layoutmode11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>layoutMode(mode: WebLayoutMode)</p>     <p>设置Web布局模式。常见问题请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/web-fit-content" target="_blank">Web组件大小自适应页面内容布局</a>。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>目前只支持两种Web布局模式，分别为Web布局跟随系统（WebLayoutMode.NONE）和Web组件高度基于前端页面高度的自适应网页布局（WebLayoutMode.FIT_CONTENT）。</p>       <p>Web组件高度基于前端页面自适应布局有如下限制：</p>       <ul>        <li>如果Web组件宽或长度超过7680px，请在Web组件创建的时候指定RenderMode.SYNC_RENDER模式，否则会整个白屏。</li>        <li>Web组件创建后不支持动态切换layoutMode模式。</li>        <li>Web组件宽高规格：指定RenderMode.ASYNC_RENDER模式时，分别不超过7680px。</li>        <li>频繁更改页面宽高会触发Web组件重新布局，影响体验。</li>        <li>不支持瀑布流网页（下拉到底部加载更多）。</li>        <li>不支持宽度自适应，仅支持高度自适应。</li>        <li>由于高度自适应网页高度，您无法通过修改组件高度属性来修改组件高度。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#weblayoutmode11">WebLayoutMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置web布局模式，跟随系统或自适应布局。</p>          <p>传入null或undefined时为WebLayoutMode.NONE。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <p>1、指明layoutMode为WebLayoutMode.FIT_CONTENT模式，为避免默认渲染模式下(RenderMode.ASYNC_RENDER)视口高度超过7680px导致页面渲染出错，需要显式指明渲染模式(RenderMode.SYNC_RENDER)。</p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#overscrollmode11">overScrollMode</a>为OverScrollMode.NEVER。</p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" <h2 id="nestedscroll11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">nestedScroll<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="nestedscroll11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>nestedScroll(value: NestedScrollOptions | NestedScrollOptionsExt)</p>     <p>调用以设置嵌套滚动选项。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>可以设置上下左右四个方向，或者设置向前、向后两个方向的嵌套滚动模式，实现与父组件的滚动联动。</li>        <li>支持嵌套滚动的容器：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-grid">Grid</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-list">List</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-scroll">Scroll</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-swiper">Swiper</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-tabs">Tabs</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-waterflow">WaterFlow</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-refresh">Refresh</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-sheet-transition#bindsheet">bindSheet</a>。</li>        <li>支持嵌套滚动的输入事件：使用手势、鼠标、触控板。</li>        <li>嵌套滚动场景下，由于Web滚动到边缘时会优先触发过滚动的过界回弹效果，建议设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#overscrollmode11">overScrollMode</a>为OverScrollMode.NEVER，避免影响此场景的用户体验。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-scrollable-common#nestedscrolloptions10对象说明">NestedScrollOptions</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#nestedscrolloptionsext14">NestedScrollOptionsExt</a><sup>14+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>可滚动组件滚动时的嵌套滚动选项。</p>          <p>value为NestedScrollOptions（向前、向后两个方向）类型时，scrollForward、scrollBackward默认滚动选项为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#nestedscrollmode10">NestedScrollMode.SELF_FIRST</a>。</p>          <p>value为NestedScrollOptionsExt（上下左右四个方向）类型时，scrollUp、scrollDown、scrollLeft、scrollRight默认滚动选项为NestedScrollMode.SELF_FIRST。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1142px;">     <h2 id="bypassvsynccondition20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">bypassVsyncCondition<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bypassvsynccondition20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>bypassVsyncCondition(condition: WebBypassVsyncCondition)</p>     <p>当开发者调用scrollBy接口进行页面滚动时，可以通过bypassVsyncCondition接口设置渲染流程跳过vsync（垂直同步）调度，直接触发绘制。该属性没有显式调用时，默认不跳过vsync调度。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">condition</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#webbypassvsynccondition20">WebBypassVsyncCondition</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>触发渲染流程跳过vsync调度的条件。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为NONE。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1022px;">     <h2 id="enablenativeembedmode11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableNativeEmbedMode<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableNativeEmbedMode(mode: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启同层渲染功能。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不开启同层渲染功能。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td id="forcedisplayscrollbar14" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">forceDisplayScrollBar<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="forcedisplayscrollbar14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>forceDisplayScrollBar(enabled: boolean)</p>     <p>设置滚动条是否常驻。在常驻状态下，当页面大小超过一页时，滚动条出现且不消失。</p>     <p>全量展开模式下不支持滚动条常驻，即layoutMode为WebLayoutMode.FIT_CONTENT模式时，参数enabled为false。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enabled</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>滚动条是否常驻。</p>          <p>true表示滚动条常驻，false表示滚动条不常驻。</p>          <p>默认值：false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3671px;">     <h2 id="registernativeembedrule12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">registerNativeEmbedRule<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="registernativeembedrule12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>registerNativeEmbedRule(tag: string, type: string)</p>     <p>注册使用同层渲染的HTML标签名和类型。标签名仅支持使用&lt;object&gt;和&lt;embed&gt;。标签类型只能使用ASCII可显示字符。</p>     <p>若指定类型与W3C定义的&lt;object&gt;或&lt;embed&gt;标准类型重合，ArkWeb内核将其识别为非同层标签。</p>     <p>本接口同样受enableNativeEmbedMode接口控制，在未使能同层渲染时本接口无效。在不使用本接口的情况下，ArkWeb内核默认将"native/"前缀类型的&lt;embed&gt;标签识别为同层标签。</p>     <p>具体使用详情请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/web-same-layer#web页面中同层渲染输入框" target="_blank">同层渲染</a>指南。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">tag</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">标签名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">标签类型，内核使用前缀匹配此参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1442px;">     <h2 id="defaulttextencodingformat12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">defaultTextEncodingFormat<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="defaulttextencodingformat12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>defaultTextEncodingFormat(textEncodingFormat: string)</p>     <p>设置网页的默认字符编码。当属性没有显式调用时，网页的默认字符编码为"UTF-8"。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">textEncodingFormat</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>默认字符编码。</p>          <p>传入null或undefined时为"UTF-8"。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!--index.html--&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">&lt;!DOCTYPE <span class="hljs-keyword">html</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">head</span>&gt;</span></li><li>    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">metaViewport<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="metaviewport12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>metaViewport(enabled: boolean)</p>     <p>设置meta标签的viewport属性是否可用。当属性没有显式调用时，默认支持meta标签的viewport属性。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当前通过User-Agent中是否含有"Mobile"字段来判断是否开启前端HTML页面中meta标签的viewport属性。当User-Agent中不含有"Mobile"字段时，meta标签中viewport属性默认关闭，此时可通过显性设置metaViewport属性为true来覆盖关闭状态。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong> 该接口在Phone、Wearable、TV设备中可正常调用，在PC/2in1设备中无效果，在Tablet设备中，设置为true或false均会解析meta标签viewport-fit属性。当viewport-fit=cover时，可通过CSS属性获取安全区域大小。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enabled</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否支持meta标签的viewport属性。</p>          <p>true表示支持meta标签的viewport属性，将解析viewport属性，并根据viewport属性布局。</p>          <p>false表示不支持meta标签的viewport属性，将不解析viewport属性，进行默认布局。</p>          <p>传入null或undefined时为true。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textAutosizing<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textautosizing12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textAutosizing(textAutosizing: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Web组件是否开启文本字体大小自动调整。当属性没有显式调用时，Web组件默认开启文本字体大小自动调整。</p>     <p>文本字体大小自动调整生效后，对于字号过小的文本将自动加大字号至16px~32px，避免屏幕较小（默认视口宽度 &lt; 980px）的设备因为缺少移动端适配出现字体过小的可读性问题。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>文本字体大小自动调整生效需要满足的前置条件：         <ul>          <li>设备形态为：Phone、Tablet、Wearable、TV。</li>          <li>Web组件视口宽度 &lt; 980px。</li>          <li>页面文本量大，页面文本的字号*字符数 ≥ 3920。</li>          <li>前端无metaViewport设置，或metaViewport设置中无"width"和"initial-scale"属性。</li>         </ul></li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong> 该接口在PC/2in1设备中无效果，在其他设备中可正常调用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">textAutosizing</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本自动调整大小。</p>          <p>true表示文本自动调整大小，false表示文本不自动调整大小。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为true。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableNativeMediaPlayer<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablenativemediaplayer12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableNativeMediaPlayer(config: NativeMediaPlayerConfig)</p>     <p>开启<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/app-takeovers-web-media" target="_blank">应用接管网页媒体播放功能</a>。当属性没有显式调用时，默认不开启接管网页媒体播放功能。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">config</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#nativemediaplayerconfig12">NativeMediaPlayerConfig</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>enable: 是否开启该功能。</p>          <p>shouldOverlay: 该功能开启后， 应用接管网页视频的播放器画面是否覆盖网页内容。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为{enable: <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1166px;">     <h2 id="onadsblocked12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onAdsBlocked<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onadsblocked12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onAdsBlocked(callback: OnAdsBlockedCallback)</p>     <p>一个页面发生广告过滤后，通过此回调接口通知过滤的详细信息。由于页面可能随时发生变化并不断产生网络请求，为了减少通知频次、降低对页面加载过程的影响，仅在页面加载完成时进行首次通知，此后发生的过滤将间隔1秒钟上报，无广告过滤则无通知。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-t#onadsblockedcallback12">OnAdsBlockedCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">广告过滤的回调。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1538px;">     <h2 id="keyboardavoidmode12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">keyboardAvoidMode<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="keyboardavoidmode12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>keyboardAvoidMode(mode: WebKeyboardAvoidMode)</p>     <p>Web组件自定义软件键盘避让模式。</p>     <p>当UIContext设置的键盘避让模式为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-e#keyboardavoidmode11">KeyboardAvoidMode.RESIZE</a>模式时，该接口功能不生效。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#webkeyboardavoidmode12">WebKeyboardAvoidMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Web软键盘避让模式。</p>          <p>嵌套滚动场景下不推荐使用web软键盘避让，包括RESIZE_VISUAL与RESIZE_CONTENT。</p>          <p>默认值：WebKeyboardAvoidMode.RESIZE_CONTENT避让行为。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!--index.html--&gt;</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">&lt;!DOCTYPE <span class="hljs-keyword">html</span>&gt;</span></li><li><span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 4202px;">     <h2 id="editmenuoptions12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">editMenuOptions<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="editmenuoptions12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>editMenuOptions(editMenu: EditMenuOptions)</p>     <p>Web组件自定义文本选择菜单。</p>     <p>用户可以通过该属性设置自定义的文本菜单。</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#oncreatemenu12">onCreateMenu</a>中，可以修改、增加、删除菜单选项，如果希望不显示文本菜单，需要返回空数组。</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#onmenuitemclick12">onMenuItemClick</a>中，可以自定义菜单选项的回调函数。该函数在菜单选项被点击后触发，并根据返回值决定是否执行系统默认的回调。返回true不执行系统回调，返回false继续执行系统回调。</p>     <p>在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#属性-1">onPrepareMenu<sup>20+</sup></a>中，当文本选择区域变化后显示菜单之前触发该回调，可在该回调中进行修改、增加、删除菜单选项，实现动态更新菜单。</p>     <p>本接口在与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#selectionmenuoptionsdeprecated">selectionMenuOptions<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>同时使用时，会使selectionMenuOptions<sup>(deprecated)</sup>不生效。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.56.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.56.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.56.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.56.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">editMenu</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#editmenuoptions">EditMenuOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Web自定义文本菜单选项。</p>          <p>菜单项数量，及菜单的content大小、icon图标尺寸，与ArkUI <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-menu">Menu</a>组件保持一致。</p>          <p>菜单中系统自带的id枚举值（<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textmenuitemid12">TextMenuItemId</a>）在Web中仅支持CUT、COPY、PASTE、SELECT_ALL、TRANSLATE、SEARCH、AI_WRITER七项。</p>          <p>onMenuItemClick函数中textRange参数在web中无意义，传入值为-1。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1442px;">     <h2 id="enablehapticfeedback13" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableHapticFeedback<sup>13+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablehapticfeedback13" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableHapticFeedback(enabled: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Web组件长按文本选择是否开启振动。需配置"ohos.permission.VIBRATE"。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enabled</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否开启振动。</p>          <p>true表示开启振动，false表示不开启振动。</p>          <p>默认值：true。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">blurOnKeyboardHideMode<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bluronkeyboardhidemode14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>blurOnKeyboardHideMode(mode: BlurOnKeyboardHideMode)</p>     <p>设置当软键盘收起时Web元素失焦模式。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-e#bluronkeyboardhidemode14">BlurOnKeyboardHideMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">设置当软键盘收起时Web元素失焦关闭或开启。默认值：BlurOnKeyboardHideMode.SILENT。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableFollowSystemFontWeight<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablefollowsystemfontweight18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableFollowSystemFontWeight(follow: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Web组件是否开启字重跟随系统设置变化。当属性没有显式调用时，Web组件默认开启字重跟随系统设置变化。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>目前该能力只支持前端文本元素跟随变化，暂不支持canvas元素、内嵌docx和pdf格式中的文本跟随变化。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.60.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">follow</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置Web组件是否开启字重跟随系统设置变化。</p>          <p>true表示字重跟随系统设置中的字体粗细变化，系统设置改变时字重跟随变化。false表示字重不再跟随系统设置中的字体粗细变化，系统设置改变时维持当前字重不变。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div </li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Entry</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Component</span></li><li>struct <span class="hljs-title class_">WebComponent</span> {</li><li>  <span class_">WebviewController</span>();</li><li>  <span class="hljs-title function_">build</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {</li><li>    <span class="hljs-title class_">Column</span>() {</li><li>      <span class="hljs-title class_">Web</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"www.example.com"</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">controller</span>: <span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">controller</span> })</li><li>        .<span class="hljs-title function_">enableFollowSystemFontWeight</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">true</span>)</li><li>    }</li><li>  }</li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1358px;">     <h2 id="optimizeparserbudget15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">optimizeParserBudget<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="optimizeparserbudget15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>optimizeParserBudget(optimizeParserBudget: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启分段解析HTML优化。当属性没有显式调用时，默认使用解析时间作为HTML分段解析的分段点。</p>     <p>ArkWeb内核在解析HTML文档结构时采取分段解析策略，旨在避免过多占用主线程资源，并使网页具有渐进式加载能力。ArkWeb内核默认使用解析时间作为分段点，当单次解析时间超过阈值时，会中断解析，随后进行布局和渲染操作。</p>     <p>开启优化后，ArkWeb内核将不仅检查解析时间是否超出限制，还会额外判断解析的Token（HTML文档的最小解析单位，例如&lt;div&gt;、attr="xxx"等）数量是否超过内核规定的阈值，并下调此阈值。当页面的FCP(First Contentful Paint 首次内容绘制）触发时会恢复成默认的中断判断逻辑。这将使得网页在FCP到来之前的解析操作更频繁，从而提高首帧内容被提前解析完成并进入渲染阶段的可能性，同时有效缩减首帧渲染的工作量，最终实现FCP时间提前。</p>     <p>由于页面的FCP触发时会恢复成默认分段解析逻辑，因此分段解析HTML优化仅对每个Web组件加载的首个页面生效。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">optimizeParserBudget</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置开启分段解析HTML优化。</p>          <p>true表示使用解析个数代替解析时间作为HTML分段解析的分段点，并减少每段解析的个数上限。false表示使用解析时间作为HTML分段解析的分段点。</p>          <p>传入undefined或null时为false。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div
