class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2002px;">     <h2 id="enabledatadetector20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableDataDetector<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enabledatadetector20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableDataDetector(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否识别网页文本特殊实体，如邮件、电话、网址等。该接口依赖设备底层具备文本识别能力，否则设置无效。</p>     <p>当enableDataDetector设置为true，同时不设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#datadetectorconfig20">dataDetectorConfig</a>属性时，默认识别所有类型的实体，所识别实体的color和decoration会被更改为如下样式：</p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'#ff0a59f7'</span>,</li><li><span class="hljs-attr">decoration</span>:{</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">TextDecorationType</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Underline</span>,</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'#ff0a59f7'</span>,</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">style</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">TextDecorationStyle</span>.<span class="hljs-property">SOLID</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>当enableDataDetector设置为true且<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#copyoptions11">copyOptions</a>设置为CopyOptions.LocalDevice时，AI菜单功能将被激活。此时，在网页中选中文本后，文本选择菜单能够展示对应的AI菜单项，包括<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textmenuitemid12">TextMenuItemId</a>中的url（打开连接）、email（新建邮件）、phoneNumber（呼叫）、address（导航至该位置）、dateTime（新建日程提醒）。</p>     <p>AI菜单生效时，需在选中范围内，包括一个完整的AI实体，才能展示对应的选项。该菜单项与<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textmenuitemid12">TextMenuItemId</a>中的askAI菜单项不同时出现。</p>     <p>示例使用场景详见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/web-data-detector" target="_blank">使用Web组件的智能分词能力</a>。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.64.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"     <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否启用Web文本识别，true表示启用，false表示不启用。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1950px;">     <h2 id="datadetectorconfig20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">dataDetectorConfig<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="datadetectorconfig20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>dataDetectorConfig(config: TextDataDetectorConfig)</p>     <p>设置文本识别配置。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#enabledatadetector20">enableDataDetector</a>一起使用，设置enableDataDetector为true时，dataDetectorConfig的配置才能生效。</p>     <p>当两个实体A、B重叠时，按以下规则保留实体：</p>     <ol>      <li>       <p>若A ⊂ B，则保留B，反之则保留A。</p></li>      <li>       <p>当A ⊄ B且B ⊄ A时，若A.start &lt; B.start，则保留A，反之则保留B。</p></li>     </ol>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.65.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.65.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.65.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.65.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">config</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textdatadetectorconfig11对象说明">TextDataDetectorConfig</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文本识别配置。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>TextDataDetectorConfig中的onDetectResultUpdate在Web组件中不支持，设置的回调不会调用。</p>       <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#copyoptions11">copyOptions</a>设置为CopyOptions.None时，TextDataDetectorConfig中的enablePreviewMenu配置项无效。</p>       <p>动态更新TextDataDetectorConfig的配置不会即时影响当前页面，需通过刷新页面来使新配置生效。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hqa-c106="" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="gesturefocusmode20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>gestureFocusMode(mode: GestureFocusMode)</p>     <p>设置Web组件手势获焦模式。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> id="forceenablezoom21" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">forceEnableZoom<sup>21+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="forceenablezoom21" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>forceEnableZoom(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Web组件是否启用强制缩放功能。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.67.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置是否遵从网页中&lt;meta name="viewport"&gt;标签设置的缩放限制。</p>          <p>设置为true时，不遵从网页缩放限制；设置为false时，遵从网页缩放限制。</p>          <p>传入undefined与null时为false。</p></td>        </tr> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">tableData</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置为true时，表示允许Web保存表单数据。</p>          <p>设置为false时，表示不允许Web保存表单数据。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 641px;">     <h2 id="wideviewmodeaccessdeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wideViewModeAccess<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wideviewmodeaccessdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>wideViewModeAccess(wideViewModeAccess: boolean)</p>     <p>设置Web是否支持html中meta标签的viewport属性。该接口为空接口。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 8开始支持，从API version 10开始废弃，并且不再提供新的接口作为替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">wideViewModeAccess</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置Web是否支持html中meta标签的viewport属性。</p>          <p>true表示支持html中meta标签的viewport属性，false表示不支持html中meta标签的viewport属性。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1750px;">     <h2 id="selectionmenuoptionsdeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">selectionMenuOptions<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="selectionmenuoptionsdeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>selectionMenuOptions(expandedMenuOptions: Array&lt;ExpandedMenuItemOptions&gt;)</p>     <p>Web组件自定义菜单扩展项接口，允许用户设置扩展项的文本内容、图标、回调方法。</p>     <p>该接口只支持选中纯文本，当选中内容包含图片及其他非文本内容时，action信息中会显示乱码。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始支持，从API version 20开始废弃。建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-attributes#editmenuoptions12">editMenuOptions<sup>12+</sup></a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Web.Webview.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">expandedMenuOptions</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-basic-components-web-i#expandedmenuitemoptions12">ExpandedMenuItemOptions</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>扩展菜单选项。</p>          <p>菜单项数量，及菜单的content大小、startIcon图标尺寸，与ArkUI <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-menu">Menu</a>组件保持一致。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>
